2227*Exodus*25*35*Bowls under two branches in three places, which together make six coming forth out of one shaft.
2228*Exodus*25*36*And both the bowls and the branches shall be of the same beaten work of the purest gold.
2229*Exodus*25*37*Thou shalt make also seven lamps, and shalt set them upon the candlestick, to give light over against.
2230*Exodus*25*38*The snuffers also and where the snuffings shall be put out, shall be made of the purest gold.
2231*Exodus*25*39*The whole weight of the candlestick with all the furniture thereof shall be a talent of the purest gold.
2232*Exodus*25*40*Look and make it according to the pattern, that was shown thee in the mount.
2233*Exodus*26*1*And thou shalt make the tabernacle in this manner: Thou shalt make ten curtains of fine twisted linen, and violet and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, diversified with embroidery.
2234*Exodus*26*2*The length of one curtain shall be twenty-eight cubits, the breadth shall be four cubits. All the curtains shall be of one measure.
2235*Exodus*26*3*Five curtains shall be joined one to another, and the other five shall be coupled together in like manner.
2236*Exodus*26*4*Thou shalt make loops of violet in the sides and tops of the curtains, that they may be joined one to another.
2237*Exodus*26*5*Every curtain shall have fifty loops on both sides, so set on, that one loop may be against another loop, and one may be fitted to the other.
2238*Exodus*26*6*Thou shalt make also fifty rings of gold wherewith the veils of the curtains are to be joined, that it may be made one tabernacle.
2239*Exodus*26*7*Thou shalt make also eleven curtains of goats' hair, to cover the top of the tabernacle.
2240*Exodus*26*8*The length of one hair curtain shall be thirty cubits: and the breadth four: the measure of all the curtains shall be equal.
2241*Exodus*26*9*Five of which thou shalt couple by themselves, and the six others thou shalt couple one to another, so as to double the sixth curtain in the front of the roof.
2242*Exodus*26*10*Thou shalt make also fifty loops in the edge of one curtain, that it may be joined with the other: and fifty loops in the edge of the other curtain, that it may be coupled with its fellow.
2243*Exodus*26*11*Thou shalt make also fifty buckles of brass, wherewith the loops may be joined, that of all there may be made one covering.
2244*Exodus*26*12*And that which shall remain of the curtains, that are prepared for the roof, to wit, one curtain that is over and above, with the half thereof thou shalt cover the back parts of the tabernacle.
2245*Exodus*26*13*And there shall hang down a cubit on the one side, and another on the other side, which is over and above in the length of the curtains, fencing both sides of the tabernacle.
2246*Exodus*26*14*Thou shalt make also another cover to the roof, of rams' skins dyed red; and over that again another cover of violet coloured skins.
2247*Exodus*26*15*Thou shalt make also the boards of the tabernacle standing upright of setim wood.
2248*Exodus*26*16*Let every one of them be ten cubits in length, and in breadth on cubit and a half.
2249*Exodus*26*17*In the sides of the boards shall be made two mortises, whereby one board may be joined to another board: and after this manner shall all the boards be prepared.
2250*Exodus*26*18*Of which twenty shall be in the south side southward.
2251*Exodus*26*19*For which thou shalt cast forty sockets of silver, that under every board may be put two sockets at the two corners.
2252*Exodus*26*20*In the second side also the tabernacle that looketh to the north, there shall be twenty boards,
2253*Exodus*26*21*Having forty sockets of silver, two sockets shall be put under each board.
2254*Exodus*26*22*But on the west side of the tabernacle thou shalt make six boards.
2255*Exodus*26*23*And again other two which shall be erected in the corners at the back of the tabernacle.
2256*Exodus*26*24*And they shall be joined together from beneath unto the top, and one joint shall hold them all. The like joining shall be observed for the two boards also that are to be put in the corners.
2257*Exodus*26*25*And they shall be in all eight boards, and their silver sockets sixteen, reckoning two sockets for each board.
2258*Exodus*26*26*Thou shalt make also five bars of setim wood, to hold together the boards on one side of the tabernacle.
2259*Exodus*26*27*And five others on the other side, and as many at the west side:
2260*Exodus*26*28*And they shall be put along by the midst of the boards from one end to the other.
2261*Exodus*26*29*The boards also themselves thou shalt overlay with gold, and shall cast rings of gold to be set upon them, for places for the bars to hold together boardwork: which bars thou shalt cover with plates of gold.
2262*Exodus*26*30*And thou shalt rear up the tabernacle according to the pattern that was shown thee in the mount.
2263*Exodus*26*31*Thou shalt make also a veil of violet and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen, wrought with embroidered work, and goodly variety:
2264*Exodus*26*32*And thou shalt hang it up before four pillars of setim wood, which themselves also shall be overlaid with gold, and shall have heads of gold, but sockets of silver.
2265*Exodus*26*33*And the veils shall be hanged on with rings, and within it thou shalt put the ark of the testimony, and the sanctuary, and the holy of holies shall be divided with it.
2266*Exodus*26*34*And thou shalt set the propitiatory upon the ark of the testimony in the holy of holies.
2267*Exodus*26*35*And the table without the veil: and over against the table the candlestick in the south side of the tabernacle; for the table shall stand in the north side.
2268*Exodus*26*36*Thou shalt make also a hanging in the entrance of the tabernacle of violet and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen with embroidered work.
2269*Exodus*26*37*And thou shalt overlay with gold five pillars of setim wood, before which the hanging shall be drawn: their heads shall be of gold, and the sockets of brass.
2270*Exodus*27*1*Thou shalt make also an altar of setim wood, which shall be five cubits long and as many broad, that is, foursquare, and three cubits high.
2271*Exodus*27*2*And there shall be horns at the four corners of the same: and thou shalt cover it with brass.
2272*Exodus*27*3*And thou shalt make for the uses thereof pans to receive the ashes, and tongs and fleshhooks, and firepans: all its vessels thou shalt make of brass.
2273*Exodus*27*4*And a grate of brass in manner of a net: at the four corners of which shall be four rings of brass,
2274*Exodus*27*5*Which thou shalt put under the hearth of the altar: and the grate shall be even to the midst of the altar.
2275*Exodus*27*6*Thou shalt make also two bars for the altar of setim wood, which thou shalt cover with plates of brass:
2276*Exodus*27*7*And thou shalt draw them through rings, and they shall be on both sides of the altar to carry it.
2277*Exodus*27*8*Thou shalt not make it solid, but empty and hollow in the inside, as it was shown thee in the mount.
2278*Exodus*27*9*Thou shalt make also the court of the tabernacle, in the south side whereof southward there shall be hangings of fine twisted linen of a hundred cubits long for one side.
2279*Exodus*27*10*And twenty pillars with as many sockets of brass, the heads of which with their engraving of silver.
2280*Exodus*27*11*In like manner also on the north side there shall be hangings of a hundred cubits long, twenty pillars, and as many sockets of brass, and their heads with their engraving of silver.
2281*Exodus*27*12*But in the breadth of the court, that looketh to the west, there shall be hangings of fifty cubits, and ten pillars, and as many sockets.
2282*Exodus*27*13*In that breadth also of the court, which looketh to the east, there shall be fifty cubits.
2283*Exodus*27*14*In which there shall be for one side hangings of fifteen cubits, and three pillars and as many sockets.
2284*Exodus*27*15*And in the other side there shall be hangings of fifteen cubits, with three pillars and as many sockets.
2285*Exodus*27*16*And in the entrance of the court there shall be made a hanging of twenty cubits of violet and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen, with embroidered work: it shall have four pillars with as many sockets.
2286*Exodus*27*17*All the pillars of the court round about shall be garnished with plates of silver, silver heads and sockets of brass.
2287*Exodus*27*18*In length the court shall take up a hundred cubits, in breadth fifty, the height shall be of five cubits, and it shall be made of fine twisted linen, and shall have sockets of brass.
2288*Exodus*27*19*All the vessels of the tabernacle for all uses and ceremonies, and the pins both of it, and of the court, thou shalt make of brass.
2289*Exodus*27*20*Command the children of Israel that they bring thee the purest oil of the olives, and beaten with a pestle: that a lamp may burn always,
2290*Exodus*27*21*In the tabernacle of the testimony without the veil that hangs before the testimony. And Aaron and his sons shall order it, that it may give light before the Lord until the morning. It shall be a perpetual observance throughout their successions among the children of Israel.
2291*Exodus*28*1*Take unto thee also Aaron thy brother with his sons, from among the children of Israel, that they may minister to me in the priest's office: Aaron, Nadab, and Abiu, Eleazar, and Ithamar.
2292*Exodus*28*2*And thou shalt make a holy vesture for Aaron thy brother for glory and for beauty.
2293*Exodus*28*3*And thou shalt speak to all the wise of heart, whom I have filled with the spirit of wisdom, that they may make Aaron's vestments, in which he being consecrated may minister to me.
2294*Exodus*28*4*And these shall be the vestments that they shall make: A rational and an ephod, a tunick and a strait linen garment, a mitre and a girdle. They shall make the holy vestments for thy brother Aaron and his sons, that they may do the office of priesthood unto me.
2295*Exodus*28*5*And they shall take gold, and violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine linen.
2296*Exodus*28*6*And they shall make the ephod of gold, and violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen, embroidered with divers colours.
2297*Exodus*28*7*It shall have the two edges joined in the top on both sides, that they may be closed together.
2298*Exodus*28*8*The very workmanship also and all the variety of the work shall be of gold, and violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen.
2299*Exodus*28*9*And thou shalt take two onyx stones, and shalt grave on them the names of the children of Israel:
2300*Exodus*28*10*Six names on one stone, and the other six on the other, according to the order of their birth.
2301*Exodus*28*11*With the work of an engraver and the graving of a jeweller, thou shalt engrave them with the names of the children of Israel, set in gold and compassed about:
2302*Exodus*28*12*And thou shalt put them in both sides of the ephod, a memorial for the children of Israel. And Aaron shall bear their names before the Lord upon both shoulders, for a remembrance.
2303*Exodus*28*13*Thou shalt make also hooks of gold.
2304*Exodus*28*14*And two little chains of the purest gold linked one to another, which thou shalt put into the hooks.
2305*Exodus*28*15*And thou shalt make the rational of judgment with embroidered work of divers colours, according to the workmanship of the ephod, of gold, violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen.
2306*Exodus*28*16*It shall be foursquare and doubled: it shall be the measure of a span both in length and in breadth.
2307*Exodus*28*17*And thou shalt set in it four rows of stones: in the first row shall be a sardius stone, and a topaz, and an emerald:
2308*Exodus*28*18*In the second a carbuncle, a sapphire and a jasper.
2309*Exodus*28*19*In the third a ligurius, an agate, and an amethyst:
2310*Exodus*28*20*In the fourth a chrysolite, an onyx, and a beryl. They shall be set in gold by their rows.
2311*Exodus*28*21*And they shall have the names of the children of Israel: with twelve names shall they be engraved, each stone with the name of one according to the twelve tribes.
2312*Exodus*28*22*And thou shalt make on the rational chains linked one to another of the purest gold:
2313*Exodus*28*23*And two rings of gold, which thou shalt put in the two ends at the top of the rational.
2314*Exodus*28*24*And the golden chains thou shalt join to the rings, that are in the ends thereof:
2315*Exodus*28*25*And the ends of the chains themselves thou shalt join together with two hooks on both sides of the ephod, which is towards the rational.
2316*Exodus*28*26*Thou shalt make also two rings of gold which thou shalt put in the top parts of the rational, in the borders that are over against the ephod, and look towards the back parts thereof.
2317*Exodus*28*27*Moreover also other two rings of gold, which are to be set on each side of the ephod beneath, that looketh towards the nether joining, that the rational may be fitted with the ephod,
2318*Exodus*28*28*And may be fastened by the rings thereof unto the rings of the ephod with a violet fillet, that the joining artificially wrought may continue, and the rational and the ephod may not be loosed one from the other.
2319*Exodus*28*29*And Aaron shall bear the names of the children of Israel in the rational of judgement upon his breast, when he shall enter into the sanctuary, a memorial before the Lord for ever.
2320*Exodus*28*30*And thou shalt put in the rational of judgment doctrine and truth, which shall be on Aaron's breast, when he shall go in before the Lord: and he shall bear the judgment of the children of Israel on his breast, in the sight of the Lord always.
2321*Exodus*28*31*And thou shalt make the tunick of the ephod all of violet,
2322*Exodus*28*32*In the midst whereof above shall be a hole for the head, and a border round about it woven, as is wont to be made in the outmost parts of garments, that it may not easily be broken.
2323*Exodus*28*33*And beneath at the feet of the same tunick round about, thou shalt make as it were pomegranates, of violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, with little bells set between:
2324*Exodus*28*34*So that there shall be a golden bell and a pomegranate, and again another golden bell and a pomegranate.
2325*Exodus*28*35*And Aaron shall be vested with it in the office of his ministry, that the sound may be heard, when he goeth in and cometh out of the sanctuary, in the sight of the Lord, and that he may not die.
2326*Exodus*28*36*Thou shalt make also a plate of the purest gold: wherein thou shalt grave with engraver's work, Holy to the Lord.
2327*Exodus*28*37*And thou shalt tie it with a violet fillet, and it shall be upon the mitre,
2328*Exodus*28*38*Hanging over the forehead of the high priest. And Aaron shall bear the iniquities of those things, which the children of Israel have offered and sanctified, in all their gifts and offerings. And the plate shall be always on his forehead, that the Lord may be well pleased with them.
2329*Exodus*28*39*And thou shalt gird the tunick with fine linen, and thou shalt make a fine linen mitre, and a girdle of embroidered work.
2330*Exodus*28*40*Moreover for the sons of Aaron thou shalt prepare linen tunicks, and girdles and mitres for glory and beauty:
2331*Exodus*28*41*And with all these things thou shalt vest Aaron thy brother, and his sons with him. And thou shalt consecrate the hands of them all, and shalt sanctify them, that they may do the office of priesthood unto me.
2332*Exodus*28*42*Thou shalt make also linen breeches, to cover the flesh of their nakedness from the reins to the thighs:
2333*Exodus*28*43*And Aaron and his sons shall use them when they shall go in to the tabernacle of the testimony, or when they approach the altar to minister in the sanctuary, lest being guilty of iniquity they die. It shall be a law for ever to Aaron, and to his seed after him.
2334*Exodus*29*1*And thou shalt also do this, that they may be consecrated to me in priesthood. Take a calf from the herd, and two rams without blemish,
2335*Exodus*29*2*And unleavened bread, and a cake without leaven, tempered with oil, wafers also unleavened anointed with oil: thou shalt make them all of wheaten flour.
2336*Exodus*29*3*And thou shalt put them in a basket and offer them: and the calf and the two rams.
2337*Exodus*29*4*And thou shalt bring Aaron and his sons to the door of the tabernacle of the testimony. And when thou hast washed the father and his sons with water,
2338*Exodus*29*5*Thou shalt clothe Aaron with his vestments, that is, with the linen garment and the tunick, and the ephod and the rational, which thou shalt gird with the girdle.
2339*Exodus*29*6*And thou shalt put the mitre upon his head, and the holy plate upon the mitre,
2340*Exodus*29*7*And thou shalt pour the oil of unction upon his head: and by this rite shall he be consecrated.
2341*Exodus*29*8*Thou shalt bring his sons also and shalt put on them the linen tunicks, and gird them with a girdle:
2342*Exodus*29*9*To wit, Aaron and his children, and thou shalt put mitres upon them: and they shall be priests to me by a perpetual ordinance. After thou shalt have consecrated their hands,
2343*Exodus*29*10*Thou shalt present also the calf before the tabernacle of the testimony. And Aaron and his sons shall lay their hands upon his head,
2344*Exodus*29*11*And thou shalt kill him in the sight of the Lord, beside the door of the tabernacle of the testimony.
2345*Exodus*29*12*And taking some of the blood of the calf, thou shalt put it upon the horns of the altar with thy finger, and the rest of the blood thou shalt pour at the bottom thereof.
2346*Exodus*29*13*Thou shalt take also all the fat that covereth the entrails, and the caul of the liver, and the two kidneys, and the fat that is upon them, and shalt offer a burnt offering upon the altar:
2347*Exodus*29*14*But the flesh of the calf and the hide and the dung, thou shalt burn abroad, without the camp, because it is for sin.
2348*Exodus*29*15*Thou shalt take also one ram upon the head whereof Aaron and his sons shall lay their hands.
2349*Exodus*29*16*And when thou hast killed him, thou shalt take of the blood thereof, and pour round about the altar:
2350*Exodus*29*17*And thou shalt cut the ram in pieces, and having washed his entrails and feet, thou shalt put them upon the flesh that is cut in pieces, and upon his head.
2351*Exodus*29*18*And thou shalt offer the whole ram for a burnt offering upon the altar: it is an oblation to the Lord, a most sweet savour of the victim of the Lord.
2352*Exodus*29*19*Thou shalt take also the other ram, upon whose head Aaron and his sons shall lay their hands.
2353*Exodus*29*20*And when thou hast sacrificed him, thou shalt take of his blood, and put upon the tip of the right ear of Aaron and of his sons, and upon the thumbs and great toes of their right hand and foot, and thou shalt pour the blood upon the altar round about.
2354*Exodus*29*21*And when thou hast taken of the blood, that is upon the altar, and of the oil of unction, thou shalt sprinkle Aaron and his vesture, his sons and their vestments. And after they and their vestments are consecrated,
2355*Exodus*29*22*Thou shalt take the fat of the ram, and the rump, and the fat that covereth the lungs, and the caul of the liver, and the two kidneys, and the fat that is upon them, and the right shoulder, because it is the ram of consecration.
2356*Exodus*29*23*And one roll of bread, a cake tempered with oil, a wafer out of the basket of unleavened bread, which is set in the sight of the Lord.
2357*Exodus*29*24*And thou shalt put all upon the hands of Aaron and of his sons, and shalt sanctify them elevating before the Lord.
2358*Exodus*29*25*And thou shalt take all from their hands, and shalt burn them upon the altar for a holocaust, a most sweet savour in the sight of the Lord, because it is his oblation.
2359*Exodus*29*26*Thou shalt take also the breast of the ram, wherewith Aaron was consecrated, and elevating it thou shalt sanctify it before the Lord, and it shall fall to thy share.
2360*Exodus*29*27*And thou shalt sanctify both the consecrated breast, and the shoulder that thou didst separate of the ram,
2361*Exodus*29*28*Wherewith Aaron was consecrated and his sons, and they shall fall to Aarons share and his sons' by a perpetual right from the children of Israel: because they are the choicest and the beginnings of their peace victims which they offer to the Lord.
2362*Exodus*29*29*And the holy vesture, which Aaron shall use, his sons shall have after him, that they may be anointed, and their hands consecrated to it.
2363*Exodus*29*30*He of his sons that shall be appointed high priest in his stead, and that shall enter into the tabernacle of the testimony to minister in the sanctuary, shall wear it seven days.
2364*Exodus*29*31*And thou shalt take the ram of the consecration, and shalt boil the flesh thereof in the holy place:
2365*Exodus*29*32*And Aaron and his sons shall eat it. The loaves also, that are in the basket, they shall eat in the entry of the tabernacle of the testimony,
2366*Exodus*29*33*That it may be an atoning sacrifice, and the hands of the offerers may be sanctified. A stranger shall not eat of them, because they are holy.
2367*Exodus*29*34*And if there remain of the consecrated flash, or of the bread till the morning, thou shalt burn the remainder with fire: they shall not be eaten, because they are sanctified.
2368*Exodus*29*35*All that I have commanded thee, thou shalt do unto Aaron and his sons. Seven days shalt thou consecrate their hands:
2369*Exodus*29*36*And thou shalt offer a calf for sin every day for expiation. And thou shalt cleanse the altar when thou hast offered the victim of expiation, and shalt anoint it to sanctify it.
2370*Exodus*29*37*Seven days shalt thou expiate the altar and sanctify it, and it shall be most holy. Every one that shall touch it shall be holy.
2371*Exodus*29*38*This is what thou shalt sacrifice upon the altar: Two lambs of a year old every day continually.
2372*Exodus*29*39*One lamb in the morning and another in the evening.
2373*Exodus*29*40*With one lamb a tenth part of flour tempered with beaten oil, of the fourth part of a hin, and wine for libation of the same measure.
2374*Exodus*29*41*And the other lamb thou shalt offer in the evening, according to the rite of the morning oblation, and according to what we have said, for a savour of sweetness:
2375*Exodus*29*42*It is a sacrifice to the Lord, by perpetual oblation unto your generations, at the door of the tabernacle of the testimony before the Lord, where I will appoint to speak unto thee.
2376*Exodus*29*43*And there will I command the children of Israel, and the altar shall be sanctified by my glory.
2377*Exodus*29*44*I will sanctify also the tabernacle of the testimony with the altar, and Aaron with his sons, to do the office of priesthood unto me.
2378*Exodus*29*45*And I will dwell in the midst of the children of Israel, and will be their God:
2379*Exodus*29*46*And they shall know that I am the Lord their God, who have brought them out of the land of Egypt, that I might abide among them, I the Lord their God.
2380*Exodus*30*1*Thou shalt make also an altar to burn incense, of setim wood.
2381*Exodus*30*2*It shall be a cubit in length, and another in breadth, that is, foursquare, and two in height. Horns shall go out of the same.
2382*Exodus*30*3*And thou shalt overlay it with the purest gold, as well as the grate thereof, as the walls round about and the horns. And thou shalt make to it a crown of gold round about,
2383*Exodus*30*4*And two golden rings under the crown on either side, that the bars may be put into them, and the altar be carried.
2384*Exodus*30*5*And thou shalt make the bars also of setim wood, and shalt overlay them with gold.
2385*Exodus*30*6*And thou shalt set the altar over against the veil, that hangeth before the ark of the testimony before the propitiatory wherewith the testimony is covered, where I will speak to thee.
2386*Exodus*30*7*And Aaron shall burn sweet smelling incense upon it in the morning. When he shall dress the lamps, he shall burn it:
2387*Exodus*30*8*And when he shall place them in the evening, he shall burn an everlasting incense before the Lord throughout your generations.
2388*Exodus*30*9*You shall not offer upon it incense of another composition nor oblation, and victim, neither shall you offer libations.
2389*Exodus*30*10*And Aaron shall pray upon the horns thereof once a year, with the blood of that which was offered for sin, and shall make atonement upon it in your generations. It shall be most holy to the Lord.
2390*Exodus*30*11*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying:
2391*Exodus*30*12*When thou shalt take the sum of the children of Israel according to their number, every one of them shall give a price for their souls to the Lord, and there shall be no scourge among them, when they shall be reckoned.
2392*Exodus*30*13*And this shall every one give that passeth at the naming, half a sicle according to the standard of the temple. A sicle hath twenty obols. Half a sicle shall be offered to the Lord.
2393*Exodus*30*14*He that is counted in the number from twenty years and upwards, shall give the price.
2394*Exodus*30*15*The rich man shall not add to half a sicle, and the poor man shall diminish nothing.
2395*Exodus*30*16*And the money received which was contributed by the children of Israel, thou shalt deliver unto the uses of the tabernacle of the testimony, that it may be a memorial of them before the Lord, and he may be merciful to their souls.
2396*Exodus*30*17*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying:
2397*Exodus*30*18*Thou shalt make also a brazen laver with its foot, to wash in: and thou shalt set it between the tabernacle of the testimony and the altar. And water being put into it,
2398*Exodus*30*19*Aaron and his sons shall wash their hands and feet in it:
2399*Exodus*30*20*When they are going into the tabernacle of the testimony, and when they are to come to the altar, to offer on it incense to the Lord,
2400*Exodus*30*21*Lest perhaps they die. It shall be an everlasting law to him, and to his seed by successions.
2401*Exodus*30*22*And the Lord spoke to Moses,
2402*Exodus*30*23*Saying: Take spices, of principal and chosen myrrh five hundred sicles, and of cinnamon half so much, that is, two hundred and fifty sicles, of calamus in like manner two hundred and fifty.
2403*Exodus*30*24*And of cassia five hundred sicles by the weight of the sanctuary, of oil of olives the measure hin:
2404*Exodus*30*25*And thou shalt make the holy oil of unction, an ointment compounded after the art of the perfumer,
2405*Exodus*30*26*And therewith thou shalt anoint the tabernacle of the testimony, and the ark of the testament,
2406*Exodus*30*27*And the table with the vessels thereof, the candlestick and furniture thereof, the altars of incense,
2407*Exodus*30*28*And of holocaust, and all the furniture that belongeth to the service of them.
2408*Exodus*30*29*And thou shalt sanctify all, and they shall be most holy: he that shall touch them shall be sanctified.
2409*Exodus*30*30*Thou shalt anoint Aaron and his sons, and shalt sanctify them, that they may do the office of priesthood unto me.
2410*Exodus*30*31*And thou shalt say to the children of Israel: This oil of unction shall be holy unto me throughout your generations.
2411*Exodus*30*32*The flesh of man shall not be anointed therewith, and you shall make none other of the same composition, because it is sanctified, and shall be holy unto you.
2412*Exodus*30*33*What man soever shall compound such, and shall give thereof to a stranger, he shall be cut off from his people.
2413*Exodus*30*34*And the Lord said to Moses: Take unto thee spices, stacte, and onycha, galbanum of sweet savour, and the clearest frankincense, all shall be of equal weight.
2414*Exodus*30*35*And thou shalt make incense compounded by the work of the perfumer, well tempered together, and pure, and most worthy of sanctification.
2415*Exodus*30*36*And when thou has beaten all into very small powder, thou shalt set of it before the tabernacle of the testimony, in the place where I will appear to thee. Most holy shall this incense be to you.
2416*Exodus*30*37*You shall not make such a composition for your own uses, because it is holy to the Lord.
2417*Exodus*30*38*What man soever shall make the like, to enjoy the smell thereof, he shall perish out of his people.
2418*Exodus*31*1*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying:
2419*Exodus*31*2*Behold, I have called by name Beseleel the son of Uri the son of Hur of the tribe of Juda,
2420*Exodus*31*3*And I have filled him with the spirit of God, with wisdom and understanding, and knowledge in all manner of work.
2421*Exodus*31*4*To devise whatsoever may be artificially made of gold, and silver, and brass,
2422*Exodus*31*5*Of marble, and precious stones, and variety of wood.
2423*Exodus*31*6*And I have given him for his companion Ooliab the son of Achisamech of the tribe of Dan. And I have put wisdom in the heart of every skillful man, that they may make all things which I have commanded thee,
2424*Exodus*31*7*The tabernacle of the covenant, and the ark of the testimony, and the propitiatory that is over it, and all the vessels of the tabernacle,
2425*Exodus*31*8*And the table and the vessels thereof, the most pure candlestick with the vessels thereof, and the altars of incense,
2426*Exodus*31*9*And of holocaust, and all their vessels, the laver with its foot,
2427*Exodus*31*10*The holy vestments in the ministry for Aaron the priest, and for his sons, that they may execute their office about the sacred things:
2428*Exodus*31*11*The oil of unction, and the incense of spices in the sanctuary, all things which I have commanded thee, shall they make.
2429*Exodus*31*12*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying:
2430*Exodus*31*13*Speak to the children of Israel, and thou shalt say to them: See that thou keep my sabbath: because it is a sign between me and you in your generations: that you may know that I am the Lord, who sanctify you.
2431*Exodus*31*14*Keep you my sabbath: for it is holy unto you: he that shall profane it, shall be put to death: he that shall do my work in it, his soul shall perish out of the midst of his people.
2432*Exodus*31*15*Six days shall you do work: in the seventh day is the sabbath, the rest holy to the Lord. Every one that shall do any work on this day, shall die.
2433*Exodus*31*16*Let the children of Israel keep the sabbath, and celebrate it in their generations. It is an everlasting covenant
2434*Exodus*31*17*Between me and the children of Israel, and a perpetual sign. For in six days the Lord made heaven and earth, and in the seventh he ceased from work.
2435*Exodus*31*18*And the Lord, when he had ended these words in mount Sinai, gave to Moses two stone tables of testimony, written with the finger of God.
2436*Exodus*32*1*And the people seeing that Moses delayed to come down from the mount, gathering together against Aaron, said: Arise, make us gods, that may go before us: for as to this Moses, the man that brought us out of the land of Egypt, we know not what has befallen him.
2437*Exodus*32*2*And Aaron said to them: Take the golden earrings from the ears of your wives, and your sons and daughters, and bring them to me.
2438*Exodus*32*3*And the people did what he had commanded, bringing the earrings to Aaron.
2439*Exodus*32*4*And when he had received them, he fashioned them by founders' work, and made of them a molten calf. And they said: These are thy gods, O Israel, that have brought thee out of the land of Egypt.
2440*Exodus*32*5*And when Aaron saw this, he built an altar before it, and made proclamation by a crier's voice, saying: Tomorrow is the solemnity of the Lord.
2441*Exodus*32*6*And rising in the morning, they offered holocausts, and peace victims, and the people sat down to eat, and drink, and they rose up to play.
2442*Exodus*32*7*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying: Go, get thee down: thy people, which thou hast brought out of the land of Egypt, hath sinned.
2443*Exodus*32*8*They have quickly strayed from the way which thou didst show them: and they have made to themselves a molten calf, and have adored it, and sacrificing victims to it, have said: These are thy gods, O Israel, that have brought thee out of the land of Egypt.
2444*Exodus*32*9*And again the Lord said to Moses: See that this people is stiffnecked:
2445*Exodus*32*10*Let me alone, that my wrath may be kindled against them, and that I may destroy them, and I will make of thee a great nation.
2446*Exodus*32*11*But Moses besought the Lord his God, saying: Why, O Lord, is thy indignation kindled against thy people, whom thou hast brought out of the land of Egypt, with great power, and with a mighty hand?
2447*Exodus*32*12*Let not the Egyptians say, I beseech thee: He craftily brought them out, that he might kill them in the mountains, and destroy them from the earth: let thy anger cease, and be appeased upon the wickedness of thy people.
2448*Exodus*32*13*Remember Abraham, Isaac, and Israel, thy servants, to whom thou sworest by thy own self, saying: I will multiply your seed as the stars of heaven: and this whole land that I have spoken of, I will give to you seed, and you shall possess it for ever.
2449*Exodus*32*14*And the Lord was appeased from doing the evil which he had spoken against his people.
2450*Exodus*32*15*And Moses returned from the mount, carrying the two tables of the testimony in his hand, written on both sides,
2451*Exodus*32*16*And made by the work of God: the writing also of God was graven in the tables.
2452*Exodus*32*17*And Josue hearing the noise of the people shouting, said to Moses: The noise of battle is heard in the camp.
2453*Exodus*32*18*But he answered: It is not the cry of men encouraging to fight, nor the shout of men compelling to flee: but I hear the voice of singers.
2454*Exodus*32*19*And when he came nigh to the camp, he saw the calf, and the dances: and being very angry, he threw the tables out of his hand, and broke them at the foot of the mount:
2455*Exodus*32*20*And laying hold of the calf which they had made, he burnt it, and beat it to powder, which he strowed into water, and gave thereof to the children of Israel to drink.
2456*Exodus*32*21*And he said to Aaron: What has this people done to thee, that thou shouldst bring upon them a most heinous sin?
2457*Exodus*32*22*And he answered him: Let not my lord be offended: for thou knowest this people, that they are prone to evil.
2458*Exodus*32*23*They said to me: Make us gods, that may go before us: for as to this Moses, who brought us forth out of the land of Egypt, we know not what is befallen him.
2459*Exodus*32*24*And I said to them: Which of you hath any gold? and they took and brought it to me: and I cast it into the fire, and this calf came out.
2460*Exodus*32*25*And when Moses saw that the people were naked, (for Aaron had stripped them by occasion of the shame of the filth, and had set them naked among their enemies,)
2461*Exodus*32*26*Then standing in the gate of the camp, he said: If any man be on the Lord's side let him join with me. And all the sons of Levi gathered themselves together unto him:
2462*Exodus*32*27*And he said to them: Thus saith the Lord God of Israel: Put every man his sword upon his thigh: go, and return from gate to gate through the midst of the camp, and let every man kill his brother, and friend, and neighbour.
2463*Exodus*32*28*And the sons of Levi did according to the words of Moses, and there were slain that day about three and twenty thousand men.
2464*Exodus*32*29*And Moses said: You have consecrated your hands this day to the Lord, every man in his son and in his brother, that a blessing may be given to you.
2465*Exodus*32*30*And when the next day was come, Moses spoke to the people: You have sinned a very great sin: I will go up to the Lord, if by any means I may be able to entreat him for your crime.
2466*Exodus*32*31*And returning to the Lord, he said: I beseech thee: this people hath sinned a heinous sin, and they have made to themselves gods of gold: either forgive them this trespass,
2467*Exodus*32*32*Or if thou do not, strike me out of the book that thou hast written.
2468*Exodus*32*33*And the Lord answered him: He that hath sinned against me, him will I strike out of my book:
2469*Exodus*32*34*But go thou, and lead this people whither I have told thee: my angel shall go before thee. And I in the day of revenge will visit this sin also of theirs.
2470*Exodus*32*35*The Lord therefore struck the people for the guilt on occasion of the calf which Aaron had made.
2471*Exodus*33*1*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying: God, get thee up from this place, thou and thy people which thou has brought out of the land of Egypt, into the land concerning which I swore to Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, saying: To thy seed I will give it.
2472*Exodus*33*2*And I will send an angel before thee, that I may cast out the Chanaanite, and the Amorrhite, and the Hethite, and the Pherezite, and the Hevite, and the Jebusite.
2473*Exodus*33*3*That thou mayst enter into the land that floweth with milk and honey. For I will not go up with thee, because thou art a stiffnecked people: lest I destroy thee in the way.
2474*Exodus*33*4*And the people hearing these very bad tidings, mourned: and no man put on his ornaments according to custom.
2475*Exodus*33*5*And the Lord said to Moses: Say to the children of Israel: Thou are a stiffnecked people; once I shall come up in the midst of thee, and shall destroy thee. Now presently lay aside thy ornaments, that I may know what to do with thee.
2476*Exodus*33*6*So the children of Israel laid aside their ornaments by mount Horeb.
2477*Exodus*33*7*Moses also taking the tabernacle, pitched it without the camp afar off, and called the name thereof, The tabernacle of the covenant. And all the people that had any question, went forth to the tabernacle of the covenant, without the camp.
2478*Exodus*33*8*And when Moses went forth to the tabernacle, all the people rose up, and every one stood in the door of his pavilion, and they beheld the back of Moses, till he went into the tabernacle.
2479*Exodus*33*9*And when he was gone into the tabernacle of the covenant, the pillar of the cloud came down, and stood at the door, and he spoke with Moses.
2480*Exodus*33*10*And all saw that the pillar of the cloud stood at the door of the tabernacle. And they stood, and worshipped at the doors of their tents.
2481*Exodus*33*11*And the Lord spoke to Moses face to face, as a man is wont to speak to his friend. And when he returned into the camp, his servant Josue the son of Nun, a young man, departed not from the tabernacle.
2482*Exodus*33*12*And Moses said to the Lord; Thou commandest me to lead forth this people: and thou dost not let me know whom thou wilt send with me, especially whereas thou hast said: I know thee by name, and thou hast found favour in my sight.
2483*Exodus*33*13*If therefore I have found favour in thy sight, show me thy face, that I may know thee, and may find grace before thy eyes: look upon thy people this nation.
2484*Exodus*33*14*And the Lord said: My face shall go before thee, and I will give thee rest.
2485*Exodus*33*15*And Moses said: If thou thyself dost not go before, bring us not out of this place.
2486*Exodus*33*16*For how shall we be able to know, I and thy people, that we have found grace in thy sight, unless thou walk with us, that we may be glorified by all people that dwell upon the earth?
2487*Exodus*33*17*And the Lord said to Moses: This word also, which thou hast spoken, will I do: for thou hast found grace before me, and thee I have known by name.
2488*Exodus*33*18*And he said: show me thy glory.
2489*Exodus*33*19*He answered: I will show thee all good, and I will proclaim in the name of the Lord before thee: and I will have mercy on whom I will, and I will be merciful to whom it shall please me.
2490*Exodus*33*20*And again he said: Thou canst not see my face: for man shall not see me and live.
2491*Exodus*33*21*And again he said: Behold there is a place with me, and thou shalt stand upon the rock.
2492*Exodus*33*22*And when my glory shall pass, I will set thee in a hole of the rock, and protect thee with my right hand, till I pass:
2493*Exodus*33*23*And I will take away my hand, and thou shalt see my back parts: but my face thou canst not see.
2494*Exodus*34*1*And after this he said: Hew thee two tables of stone like unto the former, and I will write upon them the words which were in the tables, which thou brokest.
2495*Exodus*34*2*Be ready in the morning, that thou mayst forthwith go up into mount Sinai, and thou shalt stand with me upon the top of the mount.
2496*Exodus*34*3*Let no man go up with thee: and let not any man be seen throughout all the mount: neither let the oxen nor the sheep feed over against it.
2497*Exodus*34*4*Then he cut out two tables of stone, such as had been before: and rising very early he went up into the mount Sinai, as the Lord had commanded him, carrying with him the tables.
2498*Exodus*34*5*And when the Lord was come down in a cloud, Moses stood with him, calling upon the name of the Lord.
2499*Exodus*34*6*And when he passed before him, he said: O the Lord, the Lord God, merciful and gracious, patient and of much compassion, and true,
2500*Exodus*34*7*Who keepest mercy unto thousands: who takest away iniquity, and wickedness, and sin, and no man of himself is innocent before thee. Who renderest the iniquity of the fathers to the children, and to the grandchildren, unto the third and fourth generation.
2501*Exodus*34*8*And Moses making haste, bowed down prostrate unto the earth, and adoring,
2502*Exodus*34*9*Said: If I have found grace in thy sight: O Lord, I beseech thee, that thou wilt go with us, (for it is a stiffnecked people,) and take away our iniquities and sin, and possess us.
2503*Exodus*34*10*The Lord answered: I will make a covenant in the sight of all. I will do signs such as were never seen upon the earth, nor in any nation: that this people, in the midst of whom thou art, may see the terrible work of the Lord which I will do.
2504*Exodus*34*11*Observe all things which this day I command thee: I myself will drive out before thy face the Amorrhite, and the Chanaanite, and the Hethite, and the Pherezite, and the Hevite, and the Jebusite.
2505*Exodus*34*12*Beware thou never join in friendship with the inhabitants of that land, which may be thy ruin:
2506*Exodus*34*13*But destroy their altars, break their statues, and cut down their groves:
2507*Exodus*34*14*Adore not any strange god. The Lord his name is Jealous, he is a jealous God.
2508*Exodus*34*15*Make no covenant with the men of those countries lest, when they have committed fornication with their gods, and have adored their idols, some one call thee to eat of the things sacrificed.
2509*Exodus*34*16*Neither shalt thou take of their daughters a wife for thy son, lest after they themselves have committed fornication, they make thy sons also to commit fornication with their gods.
2510*Exodus*34*17*Thou shalt not make to thyself any molten gods.
2511*Exodus*34*18*Thou shalt keep the feast of the unleavened bread. Seven days shalt thou eat unleavened bread, as I commanded thee in the time of the month of the new corn: for in the month of the springtime thou camest out from Egypt.
2512*Exodus*34*19*All of the male kind, that openeth the womb, shall be mine. Of all beasts, both of oxen and of sheep, it shall be mine.
2513*Exodus*34*20*The firstling of an ass thou shalt redeem with a sheep: but if thou wilt not give a price for it, it shall be slain. The firstborn of thy sons thou shalt redeem: neither shalt thou appear before me empty.
2514*Exodus*34*21*Six days shalt thou work, the seventh day thou shalt cease to plough, and to reap.
2515*Exodus*34*22*Thou shalt keep the feast of weeks with the firstfruits of the corn of thy wheat harvest, and the feast when the time of the year returneth that all things are laid in.
2516*Exodus*34*23*Three times in a year all thy males shall appear in the sight of the Almighty Lord the God of Israel.
2517*Exodus*34*24*For when I shall have taken away the nations from thy face, and shall have enlarged thy borders, no man shall lie in wait against thy land when thou shalt go up, and appear in the sight of the Lord thy God thrice in a year.
2518*Exodus*34*25*Thou shalt not offer the blood of my sacrifice upon leaven: neither shall there remain in the morning any thing of the victim of the solemnity of the Lord.
2519*Exodus*34*26*The first of the fruits of thy ground thou shalt offer in the house of the Lord thy God. Thou shalt not boil a kid in the milk of his dam.
2520*Exodus*34*27*And the Lord said to Moses: Write these words by which I have made a covenant both with thee and with Israel.
2521*Exodus*34*28*And he was there with the Lord forty days and forty nights: he neither ate bread nor drank water, and he wrote upon the tables the ten words of the covenant.
2522*Exodus*34*29*And when Moses came down from the mount Sinai, he held the two tables of the testimony, and he knew not that his face was horned from the conversation of the Lord.
2523*Exodus*34*30*And Aaron and the children of Israel seeing the face of Moses horned, were afraid to come near.
2524*Exodus*34*31*And being called by him, they returned, both Aaron and the rulers of the congregation. And after that he spoke to them.
2525*Exodus*34*32*And all the children of Israel came to him: and he gave them in commandment all that he had heard of the Lord in mount Sinai.
2526*Exodus*34*33*And having done speaking, he put a veil upon his face.
2527*Exodus*34*34*But when he went in to the Lord, and spoke with him, he took it away until he came forth, and then he spoke to the children of Israel all things that had been commanded him.
2528*Exodus*34*35*And they saw that the face of Moses when he came out was horned, but he covered his face again, if at any time he spoke to them.
2529*Exodus*35*1*And all the multitude of the children of Israel being gathered together, he said to them: These are the things which the Lord hath commanded to be done.
2530*Exodus*35*2*Six days you shall do work: the seventh day shall be holy unto you, the sabbath, and the rest of the Lord: he that shall do any work on it, shall be put to death.
2531*Exodus*35*3*You shall kindle no fire in any of your habitations on the sabbath day.
2532*Exodus*35*4*And Moses said to all the assembly of the children of Israel: This is the word the Lord hath commanded, saying:
2533*Exodus*35*5*Set aside with you firstfruits to the Lord. Let every one that is willing and hath a ready heart, offer them to the Lord: gold, and silver, and brass,
2534*Exodus*35*6*Violet and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine linen, goats' hair,
2535*Exodus*35*7*And rams' skins dyed red, and violet coloured skins, setim wood,
2536*Exodus*35*8*And oil to maintain lights, and to make ointment, and most sweet incense.
2537*Exodus*35*9*Onyx stones, and precious stones, for the adorning of the ephod and the rational.
2538*Exodus*35*10*Whosoever of you is wise, let him come, and make that which the Lord hath commanded:
2539*Exodus*35*11*To wit, the tabernacle and the roof thereof, and the cover, the rings, and the board work with the oars, the pillars, and the sockets:
2540*Exodus*35*12*The ark and the staves, the propitiatory, and the veil that is drawn before it:
2541*Exodus*35*13*The table with the bars and the vessels, and the loaves of proposition:
2542*Exodus*35*14*The candlestick to bear up the lights, the vessels thereof and the lamps, and the oil for the nourishing of fires:
2543*Exodus*35*15*The altar of incense, and the bars, and the oil of unction and the incense of spices: the hanging at the door of the tabernacle:
2544*Exodus*35*16*The altar of holocaust, and its grate of brass, with the bars and vessels thereof: the laver and its foot:
2545*Exodus*35*17*The curtains of the court with the pillars and the sockets, the hanging in the doors of the entry,
2546*Exodus*35*18*The pins of the tabernacle and of the court with their little cords:
2547*Exodus*35*19*The vestments that are to be used in the ministry of the sanctuary, the vesture of Aaron the high priest, and of his sons, to do the office of priesthood to me.
2548*Exodus*35*20*And all the multitude of the children of Israel going out from the presence of Moses,
2549*Exodus*35*21*Offered firstfruits to the Lord with a most ready and devout mind, to make the work of the tabernacle of the testimony. Whatsoever was necessary to the service, and to the holy vestments,
2550*Exodus*35*22*Both men and women gave bracelets and earrings, rings and tablets: every vessel of gold was set aside to be offered to the Lord.
2551*Exodus*35*23*If any man had violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, fine linen and goats' hair, rams' skins dyed red, and violet coloured skins,
2552*Exodus*35*24*Metal of silver and brass, they offered it to the Lord, and setim wood for divers uses.
2553*Exodus*35*25*The skillful women also gave such things as they had spun, violet, purple, and scarlet, and fine linen,
2554*Exodus*35*26*And goats' hair, giving all of their own accord.
2555*Exodus*35*27*But the princes offered onyx stone, and precious stones, for the ephod and the rational,
2556*Exodus*35*28*And spices and oil for the lights, and for the preparing of ointment, and to make the incense of most sweet savour.
2557*Exodus*35*29*All both men and women with devout mind offered gifts, that the works might be done which the Lord had commanded by the hand of Moses. All the children of Israel dedicated voluntary offerings to the Lord.
2558*Exodus*35*30*And Moses said to the children of Israel: Behold the Lord hath called by name Beseleel the son of Uri the son of Hur of the tribe of Juda.
2559*Exodus*35*31*And hath filled him with the spirit of God, with wisdom and understanding and knowledge and all learning.
2560*Exodus*35*32*To devise and to work in gold and silver and brass,
2561*Exodus*35*33*And in engraving stones, and in carpenters' work. Whatsoever can be devised artificially,
2562*Exodus*35*34*He hath given in his heart: Ooliab also the son of Achisamech of the tribe of Dan:
2563*Exodus*35*35*Both of them hath he instructed with wisdom, to do carpenters' work and tapestry, and embroidery in blue and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine linen, and to weave all things, and to invent all new things.
2564*Exodus*36*1*Beseleel, therefore, and Ooliab, and every wise man, to whom the Lord gave wisdom and understanding, to know how to work artificially, made the things that are necessary for the uses of the sanctuary, and which the Lord commanded.
2565*Exodus*36*2*And when Moses had called them, and every skillful man, to whom the Lord had given wisdom, and such as of their own accord had offered themselves to the making of the work,
2566*Exodus*36*3*He delivered all the offerings of the children of Israel unto them. And while they were earnest about the work, the people daily in the morning offered their vows.
2567*Exodus*36*4*Whereupon the workmen being constrained to come,
2568*Exodus*36*5*Said to Moses: The people offereth more than is necessary.
2569*Exodus*36*6*Moses therefore commanded proclamation to be made by the crier's voice: Let neither man nor woman offer any more for the work of the sanctuary. And so they ceased from offering gifts,
2570*Exodus*36*7*Because the things that were offered did suffice, and were too much.
2571*Exodus*36*8*And all the men that were wise of heart, to accomplish the work of the tabernacle, made ten curtains of twisted fine linen, and violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, with varied work, and the art of embroidering:
2572*Exodus*36*9*The length of one curtain was twenty-eight cubits, and the breadth four: all the curtains were of the same size.
2573*Exodus*36*10*And he joined five curtains, one to another, and the other five he coupled one to another.
2574*Exodus*36*11*He made also loops of violet in the edge of the curtain on both sides, and in the edge of the other curtain in like manner,
2575*Exodus*36*12*That the loops might meet on against another, and might be joined each with the other.
2576*Exodus*36*13*Whereupon also he cast fifty rings of gold, that might catch the loops of the curtains, and they might be made one tabernacle.
2577*Exodus*36*14*He made also eleven curtains of goats' hair, to cover the roof of the tabernacle:
2578*Exodus*36*15*One curtain was thirty cubits long and four cubits broad: all the curtains were of one measure.
2579*Exodus*36*16*Five of which he joined apart, and the other six apart.
2580*Exodus*36*17*And he made fifty loops in the edge of one curtain, and fifty in the edge of another curtain, that they might be joined one to another.
2581*Exodus*36*18*And fifty buckles of brass wherewith the roof might be knit together, that of all the curtains there might be made one covering.
2582*Exodus*36*19*He made also a cover for the tabernacle of rams' skins dyed red: and another cover over that of violet skins.
2583*Exodus*36*20*He made also the boards of the tabernacle of setim wood standing.
2584*Exodus*36*21*The length of one board was ten cubits: and the breadth was one cubit and a half.
2585*Exodus*36*22*There were two mortises throughout every board, that one might be joined to the other. And in this manner he made for all the boards of the tabernacle.
2586*Exodus*36*23*Of which twenty were at the south side southward,
2587*Exodus*36*24*With forty sockets of silver, two sockets were put under one board on the two sides of the corners, where the mortises of the sides end in the corners.
2588*Exodus*36*25*At that side also of the tabernacle, that looketh toward the north, he made twenty boards.
2589*Exodus*36*26*With forty sockets of silver, two sockets for every board.
2590*Exodus*36*27*But against the west, to wit, at that side of the tabernacle, which looketh to the sea, he made six boards,
2591*Exodus*36*28*And two others at each corner of the tabernacle behind:
2592*Exodus*36*29*Which were also joined from beneath unto the top, and went together into one joint. Thus he did on both sides at the corners:
2593*Exodus*36*30*So there were in all eight boards and they had sixteen sockets of silver, to wit, two sockets under every board.
2594*Exodus*36*31*He made also bars of setim wood, five to hold together the boards of one side of the tabernacle,
2595*Exodus*36*32*And five others to join together the boards of the other side: and besides these, five other bars at the west side of the tabernacle towards the sea.
2596*Exodus*36*33*He made also another bar, that might come by the midst of the boards from corner to corner.
2597*Exodus*36*34*And the board works themselves he overlaid with gold, casting for them sockets of silver. And their rings he made of gold, through which the bars might be drawn: and he covered the bars themselves with plates of gold.
2598*Exodus*36*35*He made also a veil of violet, and purple, scarlet, and fine twisted linen, varied and distinguished with embroidery:
2599*Exodus*36*36*And four pillars of setim wood, which with their heads be overlaid with gold, casting for them sockets of silver.
2600*Exodus*36*37*He made also a hanging in the entry of the tabernacle of violet, purple, scarlet, and fine twisted linen, with the work of an embroiderer.
2601*Exodus*36*38*And five pillars with their heads, which he covered with gold, and their sockets he cast of brass.
2602*Exodus*37*1*And Beseleel made also the ark of setim wood: it was two cubits and a half in length, and a cubit and a half in breadth, and the height was of one cubit and a half: and he overlaid it with the purest gold within and without.
2603*Exodus*37*2*And he made to it a crown of gold round about,
2604*Exodus*37*3*Casting four rings of gold at the four corners thereof: two rings in one side, and two in the other.
2605*Exodus*37*4*And he made bars of setim wood, which he overlaid with gold,
2606*Exodus*37*5*And he put them into the rings that were at the sides of the ark to carry it.
2607*Exodus*37*6*He made also the propitiatory, that is, the oracle, of the purest gold, two cubits and a half in length, and a cubit and a half in breadth.
2608*Exodus*37*7*Two cherubims also of beaten gold, which he set on the two sides of the propitiatory:
2609*Exodus*37*8*One cherub in the top of one side, and the other cherub in the top of the other side: two cherubims at the two ends of the propitiatory,
2610*Exodus*37*9*Spreading their wings, and covering the propitiatory, and looking one towards the other, and towards it.
2611*Exodus*37*10*He made also the table of setim wood, in length two cubits, and in breadth one cubit, and in height it was a cubit and a half.
2612*Exodus*37*11*And he overlaid it with the finest gold, and he made to it a golden ledge round about.
2613*Exodus*37*12*And to the ledge itself he made a polished crown of gold, of four fingers' breadth, and upon the same another golden crown.
2614*Exodus*37*13*And he cast four rings of gold, which he put in the four corners at each foot of the table,
2615*Exodus*37*14*Over against the crown: and he put the bars into them, that the table might be carried.
2616*Exodus*37*15*And the bars also themselves he made of setim wood, and overlaid them with gold,
2617*Exodus*37*16*And the vessels for the divers uses of the table, dishes, bowls, and cups, and censers of pure gold, wherein the libations are to be offered.
2618*Exodus*37*17*He made also the candlestick of beaten work of the finest gold. From the shaft whereof its branches, its cups, and bowls, and lilies came out:
2619*Exodus*37*18*Six on the two sides: three branches on one side, and three on the other.
2620*Exodus*37*19*Three cups in manner of a nut on each branch, and bowls withal and lilies; and three cups of the fashion of a nut in another branch, and bowls withal and lilies. The work of the six branches that went out from the shaft of the candlestick was equal.
2621*Exodus*37*20*And in the shaft itself were four cups after the manner of a nut, and bowls withal at every one, and lilies:
2622*Exodus*37*21*And bowls under two branches in three places, which together make six branches going out from one shaft.
2623*Exodus*37*22*So both the bowls, and the branches were of the same, all beaten work of the purest gold.
2624*Exodus*37*23*He made also the seven lamps with their snuffers, and the vessels where the snuffings were to be put out, of the purest gold.
2625*Exodus*37*24*The candlestick with all the vessels thereof weighed a talent of gold.
2626*Exodus*37*25*He made also the altar of incense of setim wood, being a cubit on every side foursquare, and in height two cubits: from the corners of which went out horns.
2627*Exodus*37*26*And he overlaid it with the purest gold, with its grate and the sides, and the horns.
2628*Exodus*37*27*And he made to it a crown of gold round about, and two golden rings under the crown at each side, that the bars might be put into them, and the altar be carried.
2629*Exodus*37*28*And the bars themselves he made also of setim wood, and overlaid them with plates of gold.
2630*Exodus*37*29*He compounded also the oil for the ointment of sanctification, and incense of the purest spices, according to the work of a perfumer.
2631*Exodus*38*1*He made also the altar of holocaust of setim wood, five cubits square, and three in height:
2632*Exodus*38*2*The horns whereof went out from the corners, and he overlaid it with plates of brass.
2633*Exodus*38*3*And for the uses thereof, he prepared divers vessels of brass, cauldrons, tongs, fleshhooks, pothooks, and firepans.
2634*Exodus*38*4*And he made the grate thereof of brass, in manner of a net, and under it in the midst of the altar a hearth,
2635*Exodus*38*5*Casting four rings at the four ends of the net at the top, to put in bars to carry it.
2636*Exodus*38*6*And he made the bars of setim wood, and overlaid them with plates of brass:
2637*Exodus*38*7*And he drew them through the rings that stood out in the sides of the altar. And the altar itself was not solid, but hollow, of boards, and empty within.
2638*Exodus*38*8*He made also the laver of brass, with the foot thereof, of the mirrors of the women that watch at the door of the tabernacle.
2639*Exodus*38*9*He made also the court, in the south side whereof were hangings of fine twisted linen, of a hundred cubits,
2640*Exodus*38*10*Twenty pillars of brass with their sockets, the heads of the pillars, and the whole graving of the work, of silver.
2641*Exodus*38*11*In like manner at the north side the hangings, the pillars, and the sockets and heads of the pillars were of the same measure, and work and metal.
2642*Exodus*38*12*But on that side that looketh to the west, there were hangings of fifty cubits, ten pillars of brass with their sockets, and the heads of the pillars, and all the graving of the work, of silver.
2643*Exodus*38*13*Moreover towards the east he prepared hangings of fifty cubits:
2644*Exodus*38*14*Fifteen cubits of which were on one side with three pillars, and their sockets:
2645*Exodus*38*15*And on the other side (for between the two he made the entry of the tabernacle) there were hangings equally of fifteen cubits, and three pillars, and as many sockets.
2646*Exodus*38*16*All the hangings of the court were woven with twisted linen.
2647*Exodus*38*17*The sockets of the pillars were of brass, and their heads with all their gravings of silver: and he overlaid the pillars of the court also with silver.
2648*Exodus*38*18*And he made in the entry thereof an embroidered hanging of violet, purple, scarlet, and fine twisted linen, that was twenty cubits long, and five cubits high according to the measure of all the hangings of the court.
2649*Exodus*38*19*And the pillars in the entry were four with sockets of brass, and their heads and gravings of silver.
2650*Exodus*38*20*The pins also of the tabernacle and of the court round about he made of brass.
2651*Exodus*38*21*These are the instruments of the tabernacle of the testimony, which were counted according to the commandment of Moses, in the ceremonies of the Levites, by the hand of Ithamar son of Aaron the priest:
2652*Exodus*38*22*Which Beseleel the son of Uri the son of Hur of the tribe of Juda had made as the Lord commanded by Moses,
2653*Exodus*38*23*Having for his companion Ooliab the son of Achisamech of the tribe of Dan: who also was an excellent artificer in wood, and worker in tapestry and embroidery in violet, purple, scarlet, and fine linen.
2654*Exodus*38*24*All the gold that was spent in the work of the sanctuary, and that was offered in gifts was nine and twenty talents, and seven hundred and thirty sicles according to the standard of the sanctuary.
2655*Exodus*38*25*And it was offered by them that went to be numbered, from twenty years old and upwards, of six hundred and three thousand five hundred and fifty men able to bear arms.
2656*Exodus*38*26*There were moreover a hundred talents of silver, whereof were cast the sockets of the sanctuary, and of the entry where the veil hangeth.
2657*Exodus*38*27*A hundred sockets were made of a hundred talents, one talent being reckoned for every socket.
2658*Exodus*38*28*And of the thousand seven hundred and seventy-five he made the heads of the pillars, which also he overlaid with silver.
2659*Exodus*38*29*And there were offered of brass also seventy-two thousand talents, and four hundred sicles besides.
2660*Exodus*38*30*Of which were cast the sockets in the entry of the tabernacle of the testimony, and the altar of brass with the grate thereof, and all the vessels that belong to the use thereof.
2661*Exodus*38*31*And the sockets of the court as well round about as in the entry thereof, and the pins of the tabernacle and of the court round about.
2662*Exodus*39*1*And he made, of violet and purple, scarlet and fine linen, the vestments for Aaron to wear when he ministered in the holy places, as the Lord commanded Moses.
2663*Exodus*39*2*So he made an ephod of gold, violet, and purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen.
2664*Exodus*39*3*With embroidered work: and he cut thin plates of gold, and drew them small into threads, that they might be twisted with the woof of the aforesaid colours,
2665*Exodus*39*4*And two borders coupled one to the other in the top on either side,
2666*Exodus*39*5*And a girdle of the same colours, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2667*Exodus*39*6*He prepared also two onyx stones, fast set and closed in gold, and graven by the art of a lapidary, with the names of the children of Israel:
2668*Exodus*39*7*And he set them in the sides of the ephod for a memorial of the children of Israel, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2669*Exodus*39*8*He made also a rational with embroidered work, according to the work of the ephod, of gold, violet, purple, and scarlet twice dyed, and fine twisted linen,
2670*Exodus*39*9*Foursquare, double, of the measure of a span.
2671*Exodus*39*10*And he set four rows of precious stones in it. In the first row was a sardius, a topaz, and emerald.
2672*Exodus*39*11*In the second, a carbuncle, a sapphire, and a jasper.
2673*Exodus*39*12*In the third, a ligurius, an agate, and an amethyst.
2674*Exodus*39*13*In the fourth, a chrysolite, an onyx, and a beryl, set and enclosed in gold by their rows.
2675*Exodus*39*14*And the twelve stones were engraved with the names of the twelve tribes of Israel, each one with its several name.
2676*Exodus*39*15*They made also in the rational little chains linked one to another of the purest gold,
2677*Exodus*39*16*And two hooks, and as many rings of gold. And they set the rings on either side of the rational,
2678*Exodus*39*17*On which rings the two golden chains should hang, which they put into the hooks that stood out in the corners of the ephod.
2679*Exodus*39*18*These both before and behind so answered one another, that the ephod and the rational were bound together,
2680*Exodus*39*19*Being fastened to the girdle and strongly coupled with rings, which a violet fillet joined, lest they should flag loose, and be moved one from the other, as the Lord commanded Moses.
2681*Exodus*39*20*They made also the tunick of the ephod all of violet,
2682*Exodus*39*21*And a hole for the head in the upper part at the middle, and a woven border round about the hole:
2683*Exodus*39*22*And beneath at the feet pomegranates of violet, purple, scarlet, and fine twisted linen:
2684*Exodus*39*23*And little bells of the purest gold, which they put between the pomegranates at the bottom of the tunick round about:
2685*Exodus*39*24*To wit, a bell of gold, and a pomegranate, wherewith the high priest went adorned, when he discharged his ministry, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2686*Exodus*39*25*They made also fine linen tunicks with woven work for Aaron and his sons:
2687*Exodus*39*26*And mitres with their little crowns of fine linen:
2688*Exodus*39*27*And linen breeches of fine linen:
2689*Exodus*39*28*And a girdle of fine twisted linen, violet, purple, and scarlet twice dyed, of embroidery work, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2690*Exodus*39*29*They made also the plate of sacred veneration of the purest gold, and they wrote on it with the engraving of a lapidary, The Holy of the Lord:
2691*Exodus*39*30*And they fastened it to the mitre with a violet fillet, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2692*Exodus*39*31*So all the work of the tabernacle and of the roof of the testimony was finished: and the children of Israel did all things which the Lord had commanded Moses.
2693*Exodus*39*32*And they offered the tabernacle and the roof and the whole furniture, the rings, the boards, the bars, the pillars, and their sockets,
2694*Exodus*39*33*The cover of rams' skins dyed red, and the other cover of violet skins,
2695*Exodus*39*34*The veil, the ark, the bars, the propitiatory,
2696*Exodus*39*35*The table, with the vessels thereof, and the loaves of proposition:
2697*Exodus*39*36*The candlestick, the lamps, and the furniture of them with the oil:
2698*Exodus*39*37*The altar of gold, and the ointment, and the incense of spices:
2699*Exodus*39*38*And the hanging in the entry of the tabernacle:
2700*Exodus*39*39*The altar of brass, the grate, the bars, and all the vessels thereof: the laver with the foot thereof: the hangings of the court, and the pillars with their sockets:
2701*Exodus*39*40*The hanging in the entry of the court, and the little cords, and the pins thereof. Nothing was wanting of the vessels, that were commanded to be made for the ministry of the tabernacle, and for the roof of the covenant.
2702*Exodus*39*41*The vestments also, which the priests, to wit, Aaron and his sons, used in the sanctuary,
2703*Exodus*39*42*The children of Israel offered as the Lord had commanded.
2704*Exodus*39*43*And when Moses saw all things finished, he blessed them.
2705*Exodus*40*1*And the Lord spoke to Moses, saying:
2706*Exodus*40*2*The first month, the first day of the month, thou shalt set up the tabernacle of the testimony,
2707*Exodus*40*3*And shalt put the ark in it, and shalt let down the veil before it:
2708*Exodus*40*4*And thou shalt bring in the table, and set upon it the things that are commanded according to the rite. The candlestick shall stand with its lamps,
2709*Exodus*40*5*And the altar of gold whereon the incense is burnt, before the ark of the testimony. Thou shalt put the hanging in the entry of the tabernacle,
2710*Exodus*40*6*And before it the altar of holocaust:
2711*Exodus*40*7*The laver between the altar and the tabernacle, and thou shalt fill it with water.
2712*Exodus*40*8*And thou shalt encompass the court with hangings, and the entry thereof.
2713*Exodus*40*9*And thou shalt take the oil of unction and anoint the tabernacle with its vessels, that they may be sanctified:
2714*Exodus*40*10*The altar of holocaust and all its vessels:
2715*Exodus*40*11*The laver with its foot: thou shalt consecrate all with the oil of unction, that they may be most holy.
2716*Exodus*40*12*And thou shalt bring Aaron and his sons to the door of the tabernacle of the testimony, and having washed them with water,
2717*Exodus*40*13*Thou shalt put on them the holy vestments, that they may minister to me, and that the unction of them may prosper to an everlasting priesthood.
2718*Exodus*40*14*And Moses did all that the Lord had commanded.
2719*Exodus*40*15*So in the first month of the second year, the first day of the month, the tabernacle was set up.
2720*Exodus*40*16*And Moses reared it up, and placed the boards and the sockets and the bars, and set up the pillars,
2721*Exodus*40*17*And spread the roof over the tabernacle, putting over it a cover, as the Lord had commanded.
2722*Exodus*40*18*And he put the testimony in the ark, thrusting bars underneath, and the oracle above.
2723*Exodus*40*19*And when he had brought the ark into the tabernacle, he drew the veil before it to fulfill the commandment of the Lord.
2724*Exodus*40*20*And he set the table in the tabernacle of the testimony at the north side without the veil,
2725*Exodus*40*21*Setting there in order the loaves of proposition, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2726*Exodus*40*22*He set the candlestick also in the tabernacle of the testimony over against the table on the south side,
2727*Exodus*40*23*Placing the lamps in order, according to the precept of the Lord.
2728*Exodus*40*24*He set also the altar of gold under the roof of the testimony over against the veil,
2729*Exodus*40*25*And burnt upon it the incense of spices, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2730*Exodus*40*26*And he put also the hanging in the entry of the tabernacle of the testimony,
2731*Exodus*40*27*And the altar of holocaust of the entry of the testimony, offering the holocaust, and the sacrifices upon it, as the Lord had commanded.
2732*Exodus*40*28*And he set the laver between the tabernacle of the testimony and the altar, filling it with water.
2733*Exodus*40*29*And Moses and Aaron, and his sons washed their hands and feet,
2734*Exodus*40*30*When they went into the tabernacle of the covenant, and went to the altar, as the Lord had commanded Moses.
2735*Exodus*40*31*He set up also the court round about the tabernacle and the altar, drawing the hanging in the entry thereof. After all things were perfected,
2736*Exodus*40*32*The cloud covered the tabernacle of the testimony, and the glory of the Lord filled it.
2737*Exodus*40*33*Neither could Moses go into the tabernacle of the covenant, the cloud covering all things and the majesty of the Lord shining, for the cloud had covered all.
2738*Exodus*40*34*If at any time the cloud removed from the tabernacle, the children of Israel went forward by their troops:
2739*Exodus*40*35*If it hung over, they remained in the same place.
2740*Exodus*40*36*For the cloud of the Lord hung over the tabernacle by day, and a fire by night, in the sight of all the children of Israel throughout all their mansions.
